# Introduction

Identity and constant function.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A  ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ A``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A , 0 ∙ "y" ⦂ B ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ƛ "y" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ [ 0 ∙ B ]⊸ A``

Some numbers.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 0 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ ` "z" ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 1 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · ` "z") ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , ω ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · (` "s" · ` "z")) ⦂ ℕ``

Words.

    data Mult : Set where
      0# : Mult
      1# : Mult
      ω# : Mult

# Contexts

# Properties of Vector Operations

Unit scaling does nothing.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="**-identityˡ"></a><a id="3571" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3571" class="Function">**-identityˡ</a> <a id="3584" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3586" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3588" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3589" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3589" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="3590" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3592" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3593" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="3595" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3597" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1916" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="3605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3589" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="3606" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="3611" class="Comment">-------------</a>

Scaling by a product is the composition of scalings.

Scaling the 0-vector gives the 0-vector.

Scaling by 0 gives the 0-vector.

Vector addition is commutative.

Vector addition is associative.

Scaling by a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

Scaling a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

  <a id="7095" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Linear maps preserve the 0-vector.

Adding a row of 0s to the end of the matrix and then multiplying by a vector produces a vector with a 0 at the bottom.

Multiplying by a standard basis vector projects out the corresponding column of the matrix.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⊛-identityˡ"></a><a id="10555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10555" class="Function">⊛-identityˡ</a> <a id="10567" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10569" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10571" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10572" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="10574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10574" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="10575" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10577" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10578" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10579" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10581" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10582" class="Bound">Ξ</a> <a id="10584" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2642" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="10593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10572" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="10595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10574" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="10596" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="10601" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10604" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="10606" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10608" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10572" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="10610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1716" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="10612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10578" class="Bound">A</a><a id="10613" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="10617" class="Comment">-----------------------</a>

  <a id="11209" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The standard basis vectors put together give the identity matrix.

# Simultaneous Substitution

Extend a matrix as the identity matrix -- add a zero to the end of every row, and add a new row with a 1 and the rest 0s.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="extm"></a><a id="13976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13976" class="Function">extm</a> <a id="13981" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13983" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13985" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13986" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13986" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="13988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#13988" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="13989" class="Symbol">}</a>
